### [1] [Thinking with Spatial Code for Physical-World Video Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05591)
*Jieneng Chen, Wenxin Ma, Ruisheng Yuan, Yunzhi Zhang, Jiajun Wu, Alan Yuille*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了Thinking with Spatial Code框架，将RGB视频转换为显式的、时间连贯的3D表示，用于物理世界视觉问答。该框架通过空间编码器将视频解析为结构化空间代码，使大语言模型能够直接对显式空间变量进行推理。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 当前视觉问答系统在处理物理世界场景时缺乏对3D空间结构的显式理解，难以进行几何感知的推理。本研究旨在解决RGB视频到结构化3D表示的转换问题，使大语言模型能够直接对空间变量进行推理，提升物理世界视觉问答的性能。

**Method:** 提出了Thinking with Spatial Code框架，包含空间编码器将RGB视频转换为显式的时间连贯3D表示。该编码器通过统一6D物体解析和跟踪骨干网络与几何预测来编码图像和几何特征，并进一步使用强化学习微调大语言模型，采用空间规则奖励机制鼓励视角感知和几何基础的推理。

**Result:** 该方法在VSI-Bench基准测试中超越了专有的视觉语言模型，创造了新的最先进性能。实验结果表明，提出的空间编码器能够将视频解析为具有显式3D定向边界框和语义标签的结构化空间代码，使大语言模型能够有效进行空间推理。

**Conclusion:** 该研究证明了将视频转换为显式3D空间表示的有效性，为物理世界视觉问答提供了新的解决方案。通过结合空间编码和强化学习微调，实现了大语言模型在空间推理任务上的显著提升，为多模态理解开辟了新的研究方向。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We introduce Thinking with Spatial Code, a framework that transforms RGB video into explicit, temporally coherent 3D representations for physical-world visual question answering. We highlight the empirical finding that our proposed spatial encoder can parse videos into structured spatial code with explicit 3D oriented bounding boxes and semantic labels, enabling large language models (LLMs) to reason directly over explicit spatial variables. Specifically, we propose the spatial encoder that encodes image and geometric features by unifying 6D object parsing and tracking backbones with geometric prediction, and we further finetuning LLMs with reinforcement learning using a spatial rubric reward that encourages perspective-aware, geometrically grounded inference. As a result, our model outperforms proprietary vision-language models on VSI-Bench, setting a new state-of-the-art. Code is available at https://github.com/Beckschen/spatialcode.


### [2] [From Decoupled to Coupled: Robustness Verification for Learning-based Keypoint Detection with Joint Specifications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05604)
*Xusheng Luo, Changliu Liu*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了首个用于基于热图的关键点检测器的耦合鲁棒性验证框架，该方法通过混合整数线性规划验证所有关键点的联合偏差，解决了现有解耦方法无法捕捉关键点间相互依赖性的问题。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现代神经关键点检测模型对输入扰动仍然脆弱，但由于高维输入和连续坐标输出，其形式化鲁棒性验证研究不足；现有解耦的、分类式验证方法独立验证每个关键点，忽略了关键点间的相互依赖性和下游任务需求，导致保守的保证。

**Method:** 提出首个耦合鲁棒性验证框架，将验证问题表述为使用混合整数线性规划（MILP）的证伪问题，该方法结合可达热图集合与编码联合偏差约束的多面体；不可行性证明鲁棒性，可行性提供反例，并证明该方法具有完备性：若验证模型鲁棒，则关键点检测模型保证鲁棒。

**Result:** 实验表明，耦合方法实现了高验证率，并在严格误差阈值下保持有效，而解耦方法在此条件下失效；该方法能够捕捉关键点间的相互依赖性，提供比独立验证方法更强的鲁棒性保证。

**Conclusion:** 该研究填补了关键点检测器形式化鲁棒性验证的空白，提出的耦合验证框架通过考虑关键点间的相互依赖性，为下游视觉任务提供了更实用的鲁棒性保证；该方法为关键点检测系统的安全部署奠定了基础，并可能扩展到其他连续输出视觉任务。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Keypoint detection underpins many vision tasks, including pose estimation, viewpoint recovery, and 3D reconstruction, yet modern neural models remain vulnerable to small input perturbations. Despite its importance, formal robustness verification for keypoint detectors is largely unexplored due to high-dimensional inputs and continuous coordinate outputs. We propose the first coupled robustness verification framework for heatmap-based keypoint detectors that bounds the joint deviation across all keypoints, capturing their interdependencies and downstream task requirements. Unlike prior decoupled, classification-style approaches that verify each keypoint independently and yield conservative guarantees, our method verifies collective behavior. We formulate verification as a falsification problem using a mixed-integer linear program (MILP) that combines reachable heatmap sets with a polytope encoding joint deviation constraints. Infeasibility certifies robustness, while feasibility provides counterexamples, and we prove the method is sound: if it certifies the model as robust, then the keypoint detection model is guaranteed to be robust. Experiments show that our coupled approach achieves high verified rates and remains effective under strict error thresholds where decoupled methods fail.


### [3] [DreamCAD: Scaling Multi-modal CAD Generation using Differentiable Parametric Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05607)
*Mohammad Sadil Khan, Muhammad Usama, Rolandos Alexandros Potamias, Didier Stricker, Muhammad Zeshan Afzal, Jiankang Deng, Ismail Elezi*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
DreamCAD是一个多模态生成框架，能够直接从点级监督生成可编辑的BReps而无需CAD特定标注，同时引入了包含100万+描述的CADCap-1M数据集，在多个基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有CAD生成方法受限于需要显式设计历史或BRep标签的小型标注数据集，而数百万未标注的3D网格数据未被充分利用，这限制了可扩展CAD生成的进展，因此需要开发能够利用大规模未标注数据的生成方法。

**Method:** DreamCAD将每个BRep表示为一组参数化曲面补丁（如贝塞尔曲面），并采用可微分细分方法生成网格，从而能够在3D数据集上进行大规模训练，同时重建连接且可编辑的曲面表面。

**Result:** DreamCAD在ABC和Objaverse基准测试中实现了最先进的性能，在文本、图像和点模态方面均表现出色，显著提升了几何保真度，并在用户偏好测试中获得了超过75%的偏好率。

**Conclusion:** 该研究通过利用大规模未标注数据和可微分表示方法，为可扩展CAD生成开辟了新途径，同时CADCap-1M数据集的发布将显著推动文本到CAD研究的发展，为实现无需CAD特定标注的生成模型提供了可行方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Computer-Aided Design (CAD) relies on structured and editable geometric representations, yet existing generative methods are constrained by small annotated datasets with explicit design histories or boundary representation (BRep) labels. Meanwhile, millions of unannotated 3D meshes remain untapped, limiting progress in scalable CAD generation. To address this, we propose DreamCAD, a multi-modal generative framework that directly produces editable BReps from point-level supervision, without CAD-specific annotations. DreamCAD represents each BRep as a set of parametric patches (e.g., Bézier surfaces) and uses a differentiable tessellation method to generate meshes. This enables large-scale training on 3D datasets while reconstructing connected and editable surfaces. Furthermore, we introduce CADCap-1M, the largest CAD captioning dataset to date, with 1M+ descriptions generated using GPT-5 for advancing text-to-CAD research. DreamCAD achieves state-of-the-art performance on ABC and Objaverse benchmarks across text, image, and point modalities, improving geometric fidelity and surpassing 75% user preference. Code and dataset will be publicly available.


### [4] [Adversarial Batch Representation Augmentation for Batch Correction in High-Content Cellular Screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05622)
*Lei Tong, Xujing Yao, Adam Corrigan, Long Chen, Navin Rathna Kumar, Kerry Hallbrook, Jonathan Orme, Yinhai Wang, Huiyu Zhou*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出对抗性批次表示增强（ABRA）方法，将细胞成像中的生物批次效应缓解问题构建为领域泛化任务，通过参数化特征统计量作为结构化不确定性并合成最坏情况批次扰动，在RxRx1和RxRx1-WILDS基准上实现了最先进的siRNA扰动分类性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 高内涵筛选产生的大规模细胞成像数据存在实验执行过程中的技术变异，导致生物批次效应，引发协变量偏移并降低深度学习模型在未见数据上的泛化能力。现有批次校正方法通常依赖额外先验知识或难以泛化到未见生物批次，需要更有效的解决方案。

**Method:** 本研究将生物批次缓解构建为领域泛化问题，提出对抗性批次表示增强（ABRA）方法。该方法通过参数化特征统计量作为结构化不确定性来显式建模批次间统计波动，采用最小-最大优化框架在表示空间中主动合成最坏情况生物批次扰动，并通过严格的角几何边界保持细粒度类别可区分性。为防止对抗探索过程中的表示崩溃，引入了协同分布对齐目标。

**Result:** 在大型RxRx1和RxRx1-WILDS基准上的广泛评估表明，ABRA在siRNA扰动分类任务上建立了新的最先进性能。该方法有效缓解了生物批次效应，显著提升了模型在未见批次数据上的泛化能力，超越了现有批次校正方法的性能表现。

**Conclusion:** 该研究将生物批次效应缓解重新构建为领域泛化问题，提供了一种不依赖额外先验知识的有效解决方案。ABRA通过对抗性扰动合成和几何边界约束的创新组合，在保持类别区分性的同时增强了模型对批次变化的鲁棒性，为细胞成像分析中的批次效应校正提供了新范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
High-Content Screening routinely generates massive volumes of cell painting images for phenotypic profiling. However, technical variations across experimental executions inevitably induce biological batch (bio-batch) effects. These cause covariate shifts and degrade the generalization of deep learning models on unseen data. Existing batch correction methods typically rely on additional prior knowledge (e.g., treatment or cell culture information) or struggle to generalize to unseen bio-batches. In this work, we frame bio-batch mitigation as a Domain Generalization (DG) problem and propose Adversarial Batch Representation Augmentation (ABRA). ABRA explicitly models batch-wise statistical fluctuations by parameterizing feature statistics as structured uncertainties. Through a min-max optimization framework, it actively synthesizes worst-case bio-batch perturbations in the representation space, guided by a strict angular geometric margin to preserve fine-grained class discriminability. To prevent representation collapse during this adversarial exploration, we introduce a synergistic distribution alignment objective. Extensive evaluations on the large-scale RxRx1 and RxRx1-WILDS benchmarks demonstrate that ABRA establishes a new state-of-the-art for siRNA perturbation classification.


### [5] [Post Fusion Bird's Eye View Feature Stabilization for Robust Multimodal 3D Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05623)
*Trung Tien Dong, Dev Thakkar, Arman Sargolzaei, Xiaomin Lin*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了一种后融合稳定器（PFS），这是一种轻量级模块，可在不修改现有检测器架构的情况下，通过稳定鸟瞰图特征表示来提升自动驾驶中相机-LiDAR融合检测器在域偏移和传感器故障下的鲁棒性。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 鸟瞰图融合检测器在域偏移和传感器故障下性能会显著下降，限制了自动驾驶系统在实际部署中的可靠性。现有的鲁棒性方法通常需要修改融合架构或重新训练专用模型，难以集成到已部署系统中。

**Method:** 提出后融合稳定器（PFS），这是一种轻量级模块，在现有检测器的中间鸟瞰图表示上操作，生成用于原始检测头的精炼特征图。该设计通过稳定域偏移下的特征统计、抑制受传感器退化影响的空间区域，并通过残差校正自适应恢复弱化线索，作为近似恒等变换保持性能同时提升鲁棒性。

**Result:** 在nuScenes基准测试中，PFS在多种故障模式下实现了最先进的结果，相机丢失鲁棒性提升+1.2%，低光性能提升+4.4% mAP，同时仅需3.3M参数的轻量级占用。

**Conclusion:** PFS提供了一种实用的后处理解决方案，可在不修改现有检测器架构的情况下显著提升融合系统的鲁棒性，为实际自动驾驶部署中的传感器故障和域适应问题提供了有效的轻量级解决方法。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Camera-LiDAR fusion is widely used in autonomous driving to enable accurate 3D object detection. However, bird's-eye view (BEV) fusion detectors can degrade significantly under domain shift and sensor failures, limiting reliability in real-world deployment. Existing robustness approaches often require modifying the fusion architecture or retraining specialized models, making them difficult to integrate into already deployed systems.
  We propose a Post Fusion Stabilizer (PFS), a lightweight module that operates on intermediate BEV representations of existing detectors and produces a refined feature map for the original detection head. The design stabilizes feature statistics under domain shift, suppresses spatial regions affected by sensor degradation, and adaptively restores weakened cues through residual correction. Designed as a near-identity transformation, PFS preserves performance while improving robustness under diverse camera and LiDAR corruptions. Evaluations on the nuScenes benchmark demonstrate that PFS achieves state-of-the-art results in several failure modes, notably improving camera dropout robustness by +1.2% and low-light performance by +4.4% mAP while maintaining a lightweight footprint of only 3.3 M parameters.


### [6] [Rethinking Concept Bottleneck Models: From Pitfalls to Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05629)
*Merve Tapli, Quentin Bouniot, Wolfgang Stammer, Zeynep Akata, Emre Akbas*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了CBM-Suite框架，系统解决了概念瓶颈模型的四个关键限制：概念相关性度量、线性问题、准确率差距和组件影响分析，通过熵度量、非线性层和蒸馏损失等技术实现了更准确且真正可解释的模型。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 概念瓶颈模型（CBMs）虽然基于人类可理解的概念进行预测，但面临四个基本限制：缺乏预先评估概念相关性的度量标准、导致近期CBMs完全绕过概念瓶颈的"线性问题"、与不透明模型相比存在准确率差距，以及缺乏对不同视觉主干网络和视觉语言模型影响的系统研究。

**Method:** 本文提出了CBM-Suite方法框架，首先引入基于熵的度量来量化概念集对特定数据集的固有适用性；其次通过在线性概念激活和分类器之间插入非线性层来解决线性问题，确保模型准确率真实反映概念相关性；第三采用由线性教师探针指导的蒸馏损失来缩小准确率差距；最后提供关于不同视觉编码器、视觉语言模型和概念集如何影响CBMs准确率和可解释性的综合分析。

**Result:** 广泛评估表明，CBM-Suite能够产生更准确的模型，并为改进基于概念的可解释性提供见解。该方法框架系统地解决了概念瓶颈模型的关键限制，包括概念相关性评估、线性问题缓解和准确率提升。

**Conclusion:** CBM-Suite为概念瓶颈模型提供了系统化的方法论框架，不仅解决了现有技术的关键限制，还为理解不同视觉组件如何影响概念可解释性提供了全面分析。这项工作为构建更准确且真正可解释的AI系统提供了实用指导。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) ground predictions in human-understandable concepts but face fundamental limitations: the absence of a metric to pre-evaluate concept relevance, the "linearity problem" causing recent CBMs to bypass the concept bottleneck entirely, an accuracy gap compared to opaque models, and finally the lack of systematic study on the impact of different visual backbones and VLMs. We introduce CBM-Suite, a methodological framework to systematically addresses these challenges. First, we propose an entropy-based metric to quantify the intrinsic suitability of a concept set for a given dataset. Second, we resolve the linearity problem by inserting a non-linear layer between concept activations and the classifier, which ensures that model accuracy faithfully reflects concept relevance. Third, we narrow the accuracy gap by leveraging a distillation loss guided by a linear teacher probe. Finally, we provide comprehensive analyses on how different vision encoders, vision-language models, and concept sets interact to influence accuracy and interpretability in CBMs. Extensive evaluations show that CBM-Suite yields more accurate models and provides insights for improving concept-based interpretability.


### [7] [Making Reconstruction FID Predictive of Diffusion Generation FID](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05630)
*Tongda Xu, Mingwei He, Shady Abu-Hussein, Jose Miguel Hernandez-Lobato, Haotian Zhang, Kai Zhao, Chao Zhou, Ya-Qin Zhang, Yan Wang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了插值FID（iFID），这是一种改进的重建FID变体，能够与潜在扩散模型的生成FID（gFID）强相关，解决了传统重建FID与生成FID相关性差的问题。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 当前变分自编码器（VAE）的重建FID（rFID）与潜在扩散模型的生成FID（gFID）之间存在弱相关性，这限制了rFID作为评估扩散模型生成质量的指标的有效性。本文旨在解决这一评估指标不匹配问题，并提出一种能够准确预测扩散模型生成性能的替代度量方法。

**Method:** 本文提出了插值FID（iFID），通过在潜在空间中为每个数据元素检索其最近邻，并对它们的潜在表示进行插值，然后解码插值后的潜在向量并计算解码样本与原始数据集之间的FID。该方法还深入分析了rFID与扩散细化阶段样本质量的相关性，以及iFID与扩散导航阶段样本质量的相关性，并基于扩散泛化和幻觉理论提供了理论解释。

**Result:** 实验结果表明，iFID是首个与扩散gFID表现出强相关性的度量指标，实现了约0.85的皮尔逊线性相关性和斯皮尔曼秩相关性。研究还精确界定了rFID与扩散细化阶段样本质量的相关性，以及iFID与扩散导航阶段样本质量的相关性，为不同评估指标的应用场景提供了明确指导。

**Conclusion:** iFID作为一种简单有效的评估指标，成功解决了传统重建FID与扩散模型生成性能评估不匹配的问题。该研究不仅提供了实用的评估工具，还通过理论分析揭示了重建度量与生成FID负相关的原因，为扩散模型的评估和优化提供了新的理论视角和方法论基础。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
It is well known that the reconstruction FID (rFID) of a VAE is poorly correlated with the generation FID (gFID) of a latent diffusion model. We propose interpolated FID (iFID), a simple variant of rFID that exhibits a strong correlation with gFID. Specifically, for each element in the dataset, we retrieve its nearest neighbor (NN) in the latent space and interpolate their latent representations. We then decode the interpolated latent and compute the FID between the decoded samples and the original dataset. Additionally, we refine the claim that rFID correlates poorly with gFID, by showing that rFID correlates with sample quality in the diffusion refinement phase, whereas iFID correlates with sample quality in the diffusion navigation phase. Furthermore, we provide an explanation for why iFID correlates well with gFID, and why reconstruction metrics are negatively correlated with gFID, by connecting to results in the diffusion generalization and hallucination. Empirically, iFID is the first metric to demonstrate a strong correlation with diffusion gFID, achieving Pearson linear and Spearman rank correlations approximately 0.85. The source code is provided in https://github.com/tongdaxu/Making-rFID-Predictive-of-Diffusion-gFID.


### [8] [Keeping the Evidence Chain: Semantic Evidence Allocation for Training-Free Token Pruning in Video Temporal Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05663)
*Jiaqi Li, Shuntian Zheng, Yixian Shen, Jia-Hong Huang, Xiaoman Lu, Minzhe Ni, Yu Guan*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出SemVID，一种无需训练的视觉令牌剪枝框架，用于视频时序定位任务。该框架通过保留查询关键证据和维持跨帧连接性，在显著减少视觉令牌的同时保持高定位精度，实现了精度与效率的平衡。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 视频时序定位任务需要在长视频中定位查询相关片段，现有视频语言模型计算成本过高。虽然无训练视觉令牌剪枝在视频问答中有效，但直接应用于VTG会导致性能显著下降，因为VTG依赖于边界敏感证据和跨帧推理链。

**Method:** 提出SemVID框架，基于证据保留和连接强度两个VTG特定剪枝原则。首先通过平衡查询相关性和帧间变化分配每帧令牌预算，然后选择三类令牌：用于多样化查询关键证据的对象令牌、捕捉有意义转换并作为跨帧中继的运动令牌，以及维持场景连续性的少量上下文令牌。

**Result:** 在VTG基准测试中，SemVID仅使用12.5%视觉令牌即可保留高达95.4%的mIoU，实现最高5.8倍的预填充加速。在相同预算下持续优于先前方法，实现了强大的精度-效率权衡。

**Conclusion:** 研究证明了针对特定任务设计剪枝策略的重要性，特别是对于边界敏感的视频时序定位任务。SemVID通过构建具有互补语义角色的紧凑令牌子集，为高效视频语言处理提供了有效解决方案，同时保持了跨帧推理能力。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Video Temporal Grounding (VTG) localizes the temporal boundaries of a query-relevant moment in long, untrimmed videos, making video-language-model (VLM) pipelines prohibitively expensive. While recent training-free visual token pruning has shown success in video question answering, naively applying these objectives to VTG often causes drastic degradation, as VTG crucially depends on boundary-sensitive evidence and cross-frame reasoning chains. We therefore identify two VTG-specific pruning principles: Evidence Retention (ER), which keeps query-critical patches especially around event boundaries, and Connectivity Strength (CS), which preserves token-level cross-frame connectivity for long-range evidence aggregation. Building on these insights, we propose SemVID, a training-free pruning framework that constructs a compact yet coherent token subset with complementary semantic roles. SemVID first allocates per-frame token budgets by balancing query relevance and inter-frame variation to avoid over-pruned segments, and then selects three types of tokens: object tokens for diverse query-critical evidence, motion tokens to capture meaningful transitions and serve as cross-frame relays, and a small set of context tokens for scene continuity. Extensive experiments on VTG benchmarks show that SemVID achieves a strong accuracy-efficiency trade-off, retaining up to 95.4% mIoU with only 12.5% visual tokens and delivering up to a 5.8x prefill speedup, consistently outperforming prior methods under the same budgets.


### [9] [OWL: A Novel Approach to Machine Perception During Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05686)
*Daniel Raviv, Juan D. Yepes*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了一种名为OWL的感知相关函数，旨在解决运动过程中的3D感知挑战。该函数直接从两种基本的视觉运动线索中推导数值，为每个时间点的每个点提供一组线索值，实现了无需环境先验知识的实时3D场景重建。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 本研究旨在解决运动过程中3D感知的复杂挑战，特别是如何在缺乏环境先验知识、静态环境信息或相机运动参数的情况下，仅通过视觉运动线索实现精确的3D感知。当前方法通常需要测量或已知相机与3D点之间的相对瞬时方向范围和方向平移等物理量，而OWL旨在消除这些限制，提供一种更简化的感知框架。

**Method:** OWL方法基于两种基本的视觉运动线索：固定点附近点的感知局部视觉逼近和刚性物体相对于固定点的感知旋转。该方法直接从未经处理的视觉运动图像序列中提取测量值，采用极简的基于像素的并行计算，无需显式测量相机与可见3D点之间的相对瞬时方向范围和方向平移，也不要求事先了解这些物理量的单独数值。

**Result:** 仿真实验表明，OWL能够实现3D物体随时间的几何恒常性，并仅凭视觉运动线索即可实现按比例缩放的3D场景重建。该方法在无需先验了解静态环境、运动物体或相机运动的情况下，成功获得了OWL数值，验证了其在实际应用中的可行性。

**Conclusion:** OWL提供了一种统一的、基于时间的分析方法，增强了关键的感知能力，包括按比例缩放的3D映射和相机航向估计。该方法弥合了理论概念与机器人学和自主导航实际应用之间的差距，可能为下一代自主系统的实时决策和交互提供基础构建模块，同时对自然感知、行为心理学和神经功能的理解也有潜在贡献。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We introduce a perception-related function, OWL, designed to address the complex challenges of 3D perception during motion. It derives its values directly from two fundamental visual motion cues, with one set of cue values per point per time instant. During motion, two visual motion cues relative to a fixation point emerge: 1) perceived local visual looming of points near the fixation point, and 2) perceived rotation of the rigid object relative to the fixation point. It also expresses the relation between two well-known physical quantities, the relative instantaneous directional range and directional translation in 3D between the camera and any visible 3D point, without explicitly requiring their measurement or prior knowledge of their individual values. OWL offers a unified, analytical time-based approach that enhances and simplifies key perception capabilities, including scaled 3D mapping and camera heading. Simulations demonstrate that OWL achieves geometric constancy of 3D objects over time and enables scaled 3D scene reconstruction from visual motion cues alone. By leveraging direct measurements from raw visual motion image sequences, OWL values can be obtained without prior knowledge of stationary environments, moving objects, or camera motion. This approach employs minimalistic, pixel-based, parallel computations, providing an alternative real-time representation for 3D points in relative motion. OWL bridges the gap between theoretical concepts and practical applications in robotics and autonomous navigation and may unlock new possibilities for real-time decision-making and interaction, potentially serving as a building block for next-generation autonomous systems. This paper offers an alternative perspective on machine perception, with implications that may extend to natural perception and contribute to a better understanding of behavioral psychology and neural functionality.


### [10] [MultiHaystack: Benchmarking Multimodal Retrieval and Reasoning over 40K Images, Videos, and Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05697)
*Dannong Xu, Zhongyu Yang, Jun Chen, Yingfang Yuan, Ming Hu, Lei Sun, Luc Van Gool, Danda Pani Paudel, Chun-Mei Feng*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了MultiHaystack基准测试，这是首个用于评估大规模跨模态条件下检索与推理能力的基准，揭示了当前多模态大语言模型在异构多模态检索方面的主要瓶颈。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有多模态大语言模型基准测试主要评估文本、图像或视频的单独理解能力，但忽视了从大规模异构多模态语料库中检索相关证据这一关键现实需求，大多数现有基准将检索限制在小规模单模态候选集中，过度简化了搜索空间并夸大了端到端可靠性。

**Method:** 研究者引入了MultiHaystack基准测试，该基准包含超过46,000个跨文档、图像和视频的多模态检索候选，以及747个开放但可验证的问题，每个问题都基于检索池中唯一的验证证据项，要求跨模态的证据定位和细粒度推理。

**Result:** 实验发现，当提供相应证据时模型表现良好，但从完整语料库中检索证据时性能显著下降，最强的检索器E5-V仅达到40.8%的Recall@1，而GPT-5等最先进MLLMs的推理准确率从提供证据时的80.86%降至top-5检索条件下的51.4%。

**Conclusion:** 异构多模态检索仍然是多模态大语言模型的主要瓶颈，MultiHaystack作为一个有价值的测试平台，揭示了小规模评估所掩盖的底层限制，并促进多模态系统中以检索为中心的进展。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) achieve strong performance on benchmarks that evaluate text, image, or video understanding separately. However, these settings do not assess a critical real-world requirement, which involves retrieving relevant evidence from large, heterogeneous multimodal corpora prior to reasoning. Most existing benchmarks restrict retrieval to small, single-modality candidate sets, substantially simplifying the search space and overstating end-to-end reliability. To address this gap, we introduce MultiHaystack, the first benchmark designed to evaluate both retrieval and reasoning under large-scale, cross-modal conditions. MultiHaystack comprises over 46,000 multimodal retrieval candidates across documents, images, and videos, along with 747 open yet verifiable questions. Each question is grounded in a unique validated evidence item within the retrieval pool, requiring evidence localization across modalities and fine-grained reasoning. In our study, we find that models perform competitively when provided with the corresponding evidence, but their performance drops sharply when required to retrieve that evidence from the full corpus. Additionally, even the strongest retriever, E5-V, achieves only 40.8% Recall@1, while state-of-the-art MLLMs such as GPT-5 experience a significant drop in reasoning accuracy from 80.86% when provided with the corresponding evidence to 51.4% under top-5 retrieval. These results indicate that multimodal retrieval over heterogeneous pools remains a primary bottleneck for MLLMs, positioning MultiHaystack as a valuable testbed that highlights underlying limitations obscured by small-scale evaluations and promotes retrieval-centric advances in multimodal systems.


### [11] [Interpretable Perception and Reasoning for Audiovisual Geolocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05708)
*Yiyang Su, Xiaoming Liu*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了Audiovisual Geolocation框架，通过可解释的感知和推理解决地理定位中的视觉模糊问题，结合听觉线索实现高精度全球定位。该框架包含三阶段处理流程，并在新构建的AVG基准上显著优于单模态基线方法。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 尽管多模态大语言模型在基于图像的定位方面取得进展，但精确的全球地理定位仍然面临严峻挑战，主要源于视觉景观的固有模糊性以及听觉线索的巨大潜力尚未被充分挖掘。现有方法主要依赖视觉信息，而声音景观提供的正交信号能够补充视觉模糊性，但当前缺乏系统性的视听融合定位框架。

**Method:** 本文提出三阶段视听地理定位框架：感知阶段采用混合自回归稀疏自编码器将噪声音频分解为语义基础的"声学原子"；多模态推理阶段使用通过组相对策略优化微调的MLLM将这些原子与视觉特征融合；精确预测阶段在S^2流形上应用黎曼流匹配进行最终定位。同时构建了包含20,000个剪辑、覆盖1,000个不同地点的全球尺度视频基准AVG。

**Result:** 实验结果表明，该框架在AVG基准上显著优于单模态基线方法。视听融合方法通过可解释的声音景观感知提供了关键的正交信号，结合多模态推理实现了高精度全球定位，验证了听觉线索在地理定位中的补充价值。

**Conclusion:** 研究表明声音景观的可解释感知为地理定位提供了关键的正交信号，与多模态推理结合能够显著提升定位精度。该工作不仅提出了有效的视听融合框架，还建立了首个全球尺度的视听地理定位基准，为多模态定位研究开辟了新方向，强调了跨模态信息融合在解决视觉模糊问题中的重要性。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
While recent advances in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have improved image-based localization, precise global geolocation remains a formidable challenge due to the inherent ambiguity of visual landscapes and the largely untapped potential of auditory cues. In this paper, we introduce Audiovisual Geolocation, a framework designed to resolve geographic ambiguity through interpretable perception and reasoning. We present AVG, a high-quality global-scale video benchmark for geolocation, comprising 20,000 curated clips across 1,000 distinct locations. To address the complexity of audiovisual geolocation, we propose a three-stage framework: (1) a Perception stage that utilizes a mixture-autoregressive sparse autoencoder to decompose noisy audio into semantically grounded "acoustic atoms"; (2) a Multimodal Reasoning stage that employs an MLLM finetuned via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to synthesize these atoms with visual features; and (3) a Precision Prediction stage using Riemannian Flow Matching on the $S^2$ manifold. Our experiments demonstrate that our framework significantly outperforms unimodal baselines. These results entail that interpretable perception of the soundscape provides a critical, orthogonal signal that, when coupled with multimodal reasoning, enables high-precision global localization.


### [12] [Any to Full: Prompting Depth Anything for Depth Completion in One Stage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05711)
*Zhiyuan Zhou, Ruofeng Liu, Taichi Liu, Weijian Zuo, Shanshan Wang, Zhiqing Hong, Desheng Zhang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了Any2Full，一种单阶段、领域通用且模式无关的深度补全框架，通过将补全任务重新定义为预训练单目深度估计模型的尺度提示适应，实现了对稀疏深度输入的鲁棒高效补全。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有RGBD融合深度补全方法受限于训练RGB分布和特定深度模式的联合条件学习，导致领域泛化能力不足且对多种深度模式鲁棒性有限；而基于单目深度估计模型的两阶段集成策略依赖显式的相对-度量对齐，引入了额外计算和结构化失真。

**Method:** Any2Full采用单阶段框架，将深度补全重新定义为预训练单目深度估计模型的尺度提示适应；设计了尺度感知提示编码器，从稀疏输入中提取尺度线索并编码为统一的尺度提示，引导模型生成全局尺度一致的预测同时保留其几何先验。

**Result:** 实验表明Any2Full在平均AbsREL指标上比OMNI-DC提升32.2%，在相同MDE骨干网络下比PriorDA实现1.4倍加速，在多个基准测试中展现出优越的鲁棒性和效率，建立了通用深度补全的新范式。

**Conclusion:** 该研究提出了一种无需显式对齐的单阶段深度补全方法，通过尺度提示机制有效结合了稀疏深度输入的尺度信息和预训练模型的几何先验，为跨领域、跨模式的通用深度补全提供了高效且鲁棒的解决方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Accurate, dense depth estimation is crucial for robotic perception, but commodity sensors often yield sparse or incomplete measurements due to hardware limitations. Existing RGBD-fused depth completion methods learn priors jointly conditioned on training RGB distribution and specific depth patterns, limiting domain generalization and robustness to various depth patterns. Recent efforts leverage monocular depth estimation (MDE) models to introduce domain-general geometric priors, but current two-stage integration strategies relying on explicit relative-to-metric alignment incur additional computation and introduce structured distortions. To this end, we present Any2Full, a one-stage, domain-general, and pattern-agnostic framework that reformulates completion as a scale-prompting adaptation of a pretrained MDE model. To address varying depth sparsity levels and irregular spatial distributions, we design a Scale-Aware Prompt Encoder. It distills scale cues from sparse inputs into unified scale prompts, guiding the MDE model toward globally scale-consistent predictions while preserving its geometric priors. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Any2Full achieves superior robustness and efficiency. It outperforms OMNI-DC by 32.2\% in average AbsREL and delivers a 1.4$\times$ speedup over PriorDA with the same MDE backbone, establishing a new paradigm for universal depth completion. Codes and checkpoints are available at https://github.com/zhiyuandaily/Any2Full.

#### 📄 Abstract
Video surgery timelines are an important part of tool-assisted surgeries, as they allow surgeons to quickly focus on key parts of the procedure. Current methods involve the surgeon filling out a post-operation (OP) report, which is often vague, or manually annotating the surgical videos, which is highly time-consuming. Our proposed method sits between these two extremes: we aim to automatically create a surgical timeline and narrative directly from the surgical video. To achieve this, we employ a CLIP-based multi-modal framework that aligns surgical video frames with textual gesture descriptions. Specifically, we use the CLIP visual encoder to extract representations from surgical video frames and the text encoder to embed the corresponding gesture sentences into a shared embedding space. We then fine-tune the model to improve the alignment between video gestures and textual tokens. Once trained, the model predicts gestures and phases for video frames, enabling the construction of a structured surgical timeline. ### [14] [Layer-wise Instance Binding for Regional and Occlusion Control in Text-to-Image Diffusion Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05769)
*Ruidong Chen, Yancheng Bai, Xuanpu Zhang, Jianhao Zeng, Lanjun Wang, Dan Song, Lei Sun, Xiangxiang Chu, Anan Liu*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出LayerBind，一种无需训练、即插即用的区域布局与遮挡控制方法，通过将区域生成建模为独立图层并在生成过程中绑定，实现了对文本到图像生成中区域布局和遮挡顺序的精确控制。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有区域指令布局控制方法存在两大局限：基于训练的方法继承数据偏差并降低图像质量，现有技术难以处理遮挡顺序问题，限制了实际应用。本研究旨在解决这些限制，实现精确的区域布局和遮挡控制。

**Method:** LayerBind采用两阶段方案：首先，利用多模态联合注意力中的上下文共享机制，通过图层级实例初始化创建关注各自区域的分支，在指定早期步骤按图层顺序融合形成预布局的统一潜在表示；其次，通过图层级语义护理，采用顺序分层注意力路径与标准全局路径并行运行，在图层透明度调度器下组合更新，增强区域细节并保持遮挡顺序。

**Result:** 定性和定量实验结果均证明了LayerBind的有效性，该方法在区域布局控制和遮挡顺序管理方面表现出色，展现了在创意应用中的强大潜力。该方法无需训练且即插即用，可作为跨扩散变换器的区域和遮挡控制器。

**Conclusion:** LayerBind通过重新排列早期潜在结构实现了对最终输出的有效控制，其核心洞察是空间布局和遮挡在去噪早期阶段就已确立。该方法不仅支持生成任务，还原生支持可编辑工作流程，允许灵活修改实例或重新排列可见顺序，为文本到图像生成提供了实用的区域控制解决方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Region-instructed layout control in text-to-image generation is highly practical, yet existing methods suffer from limitations: (i) training-based approaches inherit data bias and often degrade image quality, and (ii) current techniques struggle with occlusion order, limiting real-world usability. To address these issues, we propose LayerBind. By modeling regional generation as distinct layers and binding them during the generation, our method enables precise regional and occlusion controllability. Our motivation stems from the observation that spatial layout and occlusion are established at a very early denoising stage, suggesting that rearranging the early latent structure is sufficient to modify the final output. Building on this, we structure the scheme into two phases: instance initialization and subsequent semantic nursing. (1) First, leveraging the contextual sharing mechanism in multimodal joint attention, Layer-wise Instance Initialization creates per-instance branches that attend to their own regions while anchoring to the shared background. At a designated early step, these branches are fused according to the layer order to form a unified latent with a pre-established layout. (2) Then, Layer-wise Semantic Nursing reinforces regional details and maintains the occlusion order via a layer-wise attention enhancement. Specifically, a sequential layered attention path operates alongside the standard global path, with updates composited under a layer-transparency scheduler. LayerBind is training-free and plug-and-play, serving as a regional and occlusion controller across Diffusion Transformers. Beyond generation, it natively supports editable workflows, allowing for flexible modifications like changing instances or rearranging visible orders. Both qualitative and quantitative results demonstrate LayerBind's effectiveness, highlighting its strong potential for creative applications.


### [15] [Visual Words Meet BM25: Sparse Auto-Encoder Visual Word Scoring for Image Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05781)
*Donghoon Han, Eunhwan Park, Seunghyeon Seo*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了BM25-V，一种基于视觉Transformer补丁特征的稀疏自动编码器激活的稀疏图像检索方法，该方法将Okapi BM25评分应用于视觉词激活，实现了高效且可解释的检索，可作为密集重排序的高召回第一级检索器。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 密集图像检索虽然准确，但存在可解释性和归因性有限、大规模计算成本高的问题。本研究旨在开发一种既高效又具有可解释性的图像检索方法，能够在大规模场景中提供高召回率候选集，同时支持检索决策的可归因分析。

**Method:** BM25-V方法将Okapi BM25评分应用于视觉Transformer补丁特征上稀疏自动编码器产生的稀疏视觉词激活。该方法利用视觉词文档频率的高度不平衡和Zipfian分布特性，通过逆文档频率加权抑制普遍存在的低信息词，强调稀有且具有判别性的视觉词。检索过程通过稀疏倒排索引操作实现高效候选检索，并作为密集重排序的第一级检索器。

**Result:** 在七个基准测试中，BM25-V实现了Recall@200 ≥ 0.993的高召回率，使得两阶段检索流程仅需对每个查询重排序K=200个候选图像，就能在平均0.2%的误差范围内恢复接近密集检索的准确率。在ImageNet-1K上训练一次的稀疏自动编码器能够零样本迁移到七个细粒度基准测试中，无需微调，且BM25-V的检索决策可归因于具有量化IDF贡献的特定视觉词。

**Conclusion:** BM25-V证明了稀疏视觉词表示与BM25评分相结合在图像检索中的有效性，提供了一种高效、可解释且可归因的检索方法。该方法的两阶段检索架构显著降低了计算成本，同时保持了接近密集检索的准确率，为零样本跨领域检索和可解释图像检索系统提供了实用解决方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Dense image retrieval is accurate but offers limited interpretability and attribution, and it can be compute-intensive at scale. We present \textbf{BM25-V}, which applies Okapi BM25 scoring to sparse visual-word activations from a Sparse Auto-Encoder (SAE) on Vision Transformer patch features. Across a large gallery, visual-word document frequencies are highly imbalanced and follow a Zipfian-like distribution, making BM25's inverse document frequency (IDF) weighting well suited for suppressing ubiquitous, low-information words and emphasizing rare, discriminative ones. BM25-V retrieves high-recall candidates via sparse inverted-index operations and serves as an efficient first-stage retriever for dense reranking. Across seven benchmarks, BM25-V achieves Recall@200 $\geq$ 0.993, enabling a two-stage pipeline that reranks only $K{=}200$ candidates per query and recovers near-dense accuracy within $0.2$\% on average. An SAE trained once on ImageNet-1K transfers zero-shot to seven fine-grained benchmarks without fine-tuning, and BM25-V retrieval decisions are attributable to specific visual words with quantified IDF contributions.


### [16] [Spectral Probing of Feature Upsamplers in 2D-to-3D Scene Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05787)
*Ling Xiao, Yuliang Xiu, Yue Chen, Guoming Wang, Toshihiko Yamasaki*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了一种谱诊断框架，通过六个互补指标评估2D到3D重建流程中特征上采样器的三维感知能力，发现重建质量更依赖于谱结构保持而非空间细节增强。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 当前2D到3D重建流程中，特征上采样器主要关注增强空间细节（如更锐利的几何或更丰富的纹理），但其对三维感知能力的影响尚未得到充分探索，这构成了研究的核心动机。

**Method:** 本文引入了一个谱诊断框架，包含六个互补指标来表征振幅重分布、结构谱对齐和方向稳定性，并在CLIP和DINO骨干网络上对经典插值和可学习上采样方法进行了系统评估。

**Result:** 实验发现三个关键结果：结构谱一致性是新视角合成质量的最强预测因子，而高频谱斜率漂移常与重建性能负相关；几何和纹理对不同谱属性响应不同；可学习上采样器虽然产生更锐利的空间特征，但在重建质量上很少优于经典插值。

**Conclusion:** 研究表明重建质量更紧密地依赖于谱结构保持而非空间细节增强，强调谱一致性作为设计2D到3D流程中上采样策略的重要原则，为未来上采样器设计提供了新的指导方向。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
A typical 2D-to-3D pipeline takes multi-view images as input, where a Vision Foundation Model (VFM) extracts features that are spatially upsampled to dense representations for 3D reconstruction. If dense features across views preserve geometric consistency, differentiable rendering can recover an accurate 3D representation, making the feature upsampler a critical component. Recent learnable upsampling methods mainly aim to enhance spatial details, such as sharper geometry or richer textures, yet their impact on 3D awareness remains underexplored. To address this gap, we introduce a spectral diagnostic framework with six complementary metrics that characterize amplitude redistribution, structural spectral alignment, and directional stability. Across classical interpolation and learnable upsampling methods on CLIP and DINO backbones, we observe three key findings. First, structural spectral consistency (SSC/CSC) is the strongest predictor of NVS quality, whereas High-Frequency Spectral Slope Drift (HFSS) often correlates negatively with reconstruction performance, indicating that emphasizing high-frequency details alone does not necessarily improve 3D reconstruction. Second, geometry and texture respond to different spectral properties: Angular Energy Consistency (ADC) correlates more strongly with geometry-related metrics, while SSC/CSC influence texture fidelity slightly more than geometric accuracy. Third, although learnable upsamplers often produce sharper spatial features, they rarely outperform classical interpolation in reconstruction quality, and their effectiveness depends on the reconstruction model. Overall, our results indicate that reconstruction quality is more closely related to preserving spectral structure than to enhancing spatial detail, highlighting spectral consistency as an important principle for designing upsampling strategies in 2D-to-3D pipelines.

#### 📘 Detailed Summary

**Method:** 本文提出潜在帧间剪枝与注意力恢复框架，通过检测并跳过重复潜在补丁的重新计算来减少计算量，并引入新颖的注意力恢复机制来近似被剪枝token的注意力值，从而消除简单应用剪枝方法产生的视觉伪影。

**Result:** 实验表明该方法平均将视频编辑吞吐量提升1.45倍，在NVIDIA A6000上达到12.2 FPS，而基线仅为8.4 FPS，且不损害生成质量，无需额外训练即可与模型无缝集成。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Current video generation models suffer from high computational latency, making real-time applications prohibitively costly. In this paper, we address this limitation by exploiting the temporal redundancy inherent in video latent patches. To this end, we propose the Latent Inter-frame Pruning with Attention Recovery (LIPAR) framework, which detects and skips recomputing duplicated latent patches. Additionally, we introduce a novel Attention Recovery mechanism that approximates the attention values of pruned tokens, thereby removing visual artifacts arising from naively applying the pruning method. Empirically, our method increases video editing throughput by $1.45\times$, on average achieving 12.2 FPS on an NVIDIA A6000 compared to the baseline 8.4 FPS. The proposed method does not compromise generation quality and can be seamlessly integrated with the model without additional training. Our approach effectively bridges the gap between traditional compression algorithms and modern generative pipelines.


### [18] [Margin and Consistency Supervision for Calibrated and Robust Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05812)
*Salim Khazem*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了一种名为Margin and Consistency Supervision (MaCS)的简单正则化框架，通过联合实施logit空间分离和局部预测稳定性，显著提升了深度视觉分类器的校准性和分布偏移鲁棒性，同时保持或提高分类精度。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 深度视觉分类器通常能够实现高准确率，但在小分布偏移下往往校准性差且脆弱，这限制了其在现实世界应用中的可靠性。现有方法在同时提升校准性、鲁棒性和准确性方面存在不足，需要一种无需额外数据或架构修改的通用解决方案。

**Method:** 本文提出了Margin and Consistency Supervision (MaCS)框架，这是一种架构无关的正则化方法，通过两个核心组件增强交叉熵损失：一是hinge-squared边缘惩罚项，强制正确类别与最强竞争类别之间保持目标logit间隔；二是基于KL散度的正则化器，最小化干净输入与轻微扰动视图之间的预测差异，从而联合优化分类边缘和局部稳定性。

**Result:** 在多个图像分类基准测试和包括CNN与Vision Transformer在内的多种骨干网络上，MaCS一致性地改善了校准性（更低的ECE和NLL）和对常见损坏的鲁棒性，同时保持或提高了top-1准确率。该方法无需额外数据、架构修改，且推理开销可忽略不计。

**Conclusion:** MaCS提供了一种理论上有保证的实用方法，通过同时增加分类边缘和减少局部敏感性来提升泛化性能和鲁棒性边界。该框架可作为标准训练目标的有效替代方案，为构建更可靠、更鲁棒的视觉分类器提供了简单而强大的工具。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Deep vision classifiers often achieve high accuracy while remaining poorly calibrated and fragile under small distribution shifts. We present Margin and Consistency Supervision (MaCS), a simple, architecture-agnostic regularization framework that jointly enforces logit-space separation and local prediction stability. MaCS augments cross-entropy with (i) a hinge-squared margin penalty that enforces a target logit gap between the correct class and the strongest competitor, and (ii) a consistency regularizer that minimizes the KL divergence between predictions on clean inputs and mildly perturbed views. We provide a unifying theoretical analysis showing that increasing classification margin while reducing local sensitivity formalized via a Lipschitz-type stability proxy yields improved generalization guarantees and a provable robustness radius bound scaling with the margin-to-sensitivity ratio. Across several image classification benchmarks and several backbones spanning CNNs and Vision Transformers, MaCS consistently improves calibration (lower ECE and NLL) and robustness to common corruptions while preserving or improving top-1 accuracy. Our approach requires no additional data, no architectural changes, and negligible inference overhead, making it an effective drop-in replacement for standard training objectives.


### [19] [Cog2Gen3D: Sculpturing 3D Semantic-Geometric Cognition for 3D Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05845)
*Haonan Wang, Hanyu Zhou, Haoyue Liu, Tao Gu, Luxin Yan*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出Cog2Gen3D，一种基于三维认知引导的扩散框架，通过融合语义与绝对几何信息实现物理合理的3D生成。该方法构建双流语义-几何图并通过交叉注意力融合，显著提升了生成结果的语义保真度和几何合理性。

#### 📘 Detailed Summary

**Method:** 提出Cog2Gen3D框架，包含三个核心设计：认知特征嵌入将多模态信息编码为语义、几何和逻辑表示；三维潜在认知图构建双流语义-几何图并通过公共基础的交叉注意力融合；认知引导潜在扩散利用融合后的3D认知图作为条件指导3D高斯的潜在扩散生成过程。

**Result:** 在基于Marble World Labs构建的验证子集上进行广泛实验，Cog2Gen3D在语义保真度和几何合理性方面显著优于现有方法。统一的3D认知图框架确保了生成结果的物理合理性和结构合理性。

**Conclusion:** 研究表明语义信息与绝对几何的融合对于三维认知至关重要，能够实现物理世界的可控3D生成。提出的认知引导扩散框架为3D生成提供了新的方向，通过结构化表示融合解决了现有方法的尺度不一致问题。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Generative models have achieved success in producing semantically plausible 2D images, but it remains challenging in 3D generation due to the absence of spatial geometry constraints. Typically, existing methods utilize geometric features as conditions to enhance spatial awareness. However, these methods can only model relative relationships and are prone to scale inconsistency of absolute geometry. Thus, we argue that semantic information and absolute geometry empower 3D cognition, thereby enabling controllable 3D generation for the physical world. In this work, we propose Cog2Gen3D, a 3D cognition-guided diffusion framework for 3D generation. Our model is guided by three key designs: 1) Cognitive Feature Embeddings. We encode different modalities into semantic and geometric representations and further extract logical representations. 2) 3D Latent Cognition Graph. We structure different representations into dual-stream semantic-geometric graphs and fuse them via common-based cross-attention to obtain a 3D cognition graph. 3) Cognition-Guided Latent Diffusion. We leverage the fused 3D cognition graph as the condition to guide the latent diffusion process for 3D Gaussian generation. Under this unified framework, the 3D cognition graph ensures the physical plausibility and structural rationality of 3D generation. Moreover, we construct a validation subset based on the Marble World Labs. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our Cog2Gen3D significantly outperforms existing methods in both semantic fidelity and geometric plausibility.

**Result:** 该方法在复杂病灶分割任务中取得了最先进的结果，平均Dice系数达到37.06%，比次优基线高出14.89%，同时将失败率降低至18.42%，显著提升了分割性能和推理能力。

**Conclusion:** 该研究展示了推理与分割集成的有效性，为医学图像分析提供了新的认知推理范式，通过思维链基准和自适应训练策略解决了复杂病灶分割中的专业视觉推理挑战，为未来可解释医学AI系统的发展指明了方向。

#### 📄 Abstract
Medical image segmentation is undergoing a paradigm shift from conventional visual pattern matching to cognitive reasoning analysis. Although Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown promise in integrating linguistic and visual knowledge, significant gaps remain: existing general MLLMs possess broad common sense but lack the specialized visual reasoning required for complex lesions, whereas traditional segmentation models excel at pixel-level segmentation but lack logical interpretability. In this paper, we introduce ComLesion-14K, the first diverse Chain-of-Thought (CoT) benchmark for reasoning-driven complex lesion segmentation. To accomplish this task, we propose CORE-Seg, an end-to-end framework integrating reasoning with segmentation through a Semantic-Guided Prompt Adapter. We design a progressive training strategy from SFT to GRPO, equipped with an adaptive dual-granularity reward mechanism to mitigate reward sparsity. Our Method achieves state-of-the-art results with a mean Dice of 37.06\% (14.89\% higher than the second-best baseline), while reducing the failure rate to 18.42\%. ### [21] [VS3R: Robust Full-frame Video Stabilization via Deep 3D Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05851)
*Muhua Zhu, Xinhao Jin, Yu Zhang, Yifei Xue, Tie Ji, Yizhen Lao*

#### 📘 Detailed Summary

**Method:** VS3R框架协同整合前馈式3D重建与生成式视频扩散技术，通过联合估计相机参数、深度和掩码确保全场景可靠性，引入混合稳定渲染模块融合语义与几何线索以保持动态一致性，并采用双流视频扩散模型通过结构引导与语义锚点的协同作用修复遮挡区域和校正伪影。

**Result:** VS3R在多种相机模型上实现了高保真度的全帧稳定效果，在鲁棒性和视觉质量方面显著优于现有最先进方法。实验表明该框架能够有效处理极端运动情况，同时保持视频内容的完整性和自然性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究证明了将3D重建与生成式扩散模型协同整合的有效性，为视频稳定化提供了兼顾几何准确性与视觉一致性的新范式。框架的成功表明语义-几何融合与生成式修复的结合能够突破传统方法的局限性，为未来视频处理技术的发展提供了重要方向。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Video stabilization aims to mitigate camera shake but faces a fundamental trade-off between geometric robustness and full-frame consistency. While 2D methods suffer from aggressive cropping, 3D techniques are often undermined by fragile optimization pipelines that fail under extreme motions. To bridge this gap, we propose VS3R, a framework that synergizes feed-forward 3D reconstruction with generative video diffusion. Our pipeline jointly estimates camera parameters, depth, and masks to ensure all-scenario reliability, and introduces a Hybrid Stabilized Rendering module that fuses semantic and geometric cues for dynamic consistency. Finally, a Dual-Stream Video Diffusion Model restores disoccluded regions and rectifies artifacts by synergizing structural guidance with semantic anchors. Collectively, VS3R achieves high-fidelity, full-frame stabilization across diverse camera models and significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods in robustness and visual quality.


### [22] [BlackMirror: Black-Box Backdoor Detection for Text-to-Image Models via Instruction-Response Deviation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05921)
*Feiran Li, Qianqian Xu, Shilong Bao, Zhiyong Yang, Xilin Zhao, Xiaochun Cao, Qingming Huang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出BlackMirror框架，用于在黑盒设置下检测后门文本到图像模型。该框架基于一个关键观察：后门攻击中只有部分语义模式被稳定操纵，而其余内容保持多样或良性，从而实现了对视觉多样后门生成的准确检测。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有后门检测方法通常依赖图像级相似性分析，假设后门触发生成具有强一致性，但难以泛化到新兴的后门攻击，其中后门生成可能呈现视觉多样性。本文旨在解决在黑盒设置下检测这些视觉多样后门文本到图像模型的挑战。

**Method:** BlackMirror框架包含两个核心组件：MirrorMatch将视觉模式与相应指令对齐以检测语义偏差；MirrorVerify评估这些偏差在不同提示下的稳定性以区分真实后门行为与良性响应。这是一个无需训练、即插即用的通用框架，可部署在模型即服务应用中。

**Result:** 综合实验表明，BlackMirror在广泛的攻击范围内实现了准确检测。该框架在各种后门攻击场景下表现出色，验证了其基于部分语义模式稳定操纵观察的有效性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究揭示了后门攻击中部分语义模式稳定操纵的关键特性，为黑盒后门检测提供了新视角。BlackMirror作为一个通用、无需训练的框架，为模型即服务应用中的安全检测提供了实用解决方案，并开源代码促进进一步研究。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
This paper investigates the challenging task of detecting backdoored text-to-image models under black-box settings and introduces a novel detection framework BlackMirror. Existing approaches typically rely on analyzing image-level similarity, under the assumption that backdoor-triggered generations exhibit strong consistency across samples. However, they struggle to generalize to recently emerging backdoor attacks, where backdoored generations can appear visually diverse. BlackMirror is motivated by an observation: across backdoor attacks, {only partial semantic patterns within the generated image are steadily manipulated, while the rest of the content remains diverse or benign. Accordingly, BlackMirror consists of two components: MirrorMatch, which aligns visual patterns with the corresponding instructions to detect semantic deviations; and MirrorVerify, which evaluates the stability of these deviations across varied prompts to distinguish true backdoor behavior from benign responses. BlackMirror is a general, training-free framework that can be deployed as a plug-and-play module in Model-as-a-Service (MaaS) applications. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate that BlackMirror achieves accurate detection across a wide range of attacks. Code is available at https://github.com/Ferry-Li/BlackMirror.

#### 📄 Abstract
Accurate tumor analysis is central to clinical radiology and precision oncology, where early detection, reliable lesion characterization, and pathology-level risk assessment guide diagnosis and treatment planning. Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning is particularly important in this setting because it enables step-by-step interpretation from imaging findings to clinical impressions and pathology conclusions, improving traceability and reducing diagnostic errors. Here, we target the clinical tumor analysis task and build a large-scale benchmark that operationalizes a multimodal reasoning pipeline, spanning findings, impressions, and pathology predictions. We curate TumorCoT, a large-scale dataset of 1.5M CoT-labeled VQA instructions paired with 3D CT scans, with step-aligned rationales and cross-modal alignments along the trajectory from findings to impression to pathology, enabling evaluation of both answer accuracy and reasoning consistency. We further propose TumorChain, a multimodal interleaved reasoning framework that tightly couples 3D imaging encoders, clinical text understanding, and organ-level vision-language alignment. Through cross-modal alignment and iterative interleaved causal reasoning, TumorChain grounds visual evidence, aggregates conclusions, and issues pathology predictions after multiple rounds of self-refinement, improving traceability and reducing hallucination risk. Experiments show consistent improvements over strong baselines in lesion detection, impression generation, and pathology classification, and demonstrate strong generalization on the DeepTumorVQA benchmark. These results highlight the potential of multimodal reasoning for reliable and interpretable tumor analysis in clinical practice. Detailed information about our project can be found on our project homepage at https://github.com/ZJU4HealthCare/TumorChain.


### [24] [Energy-Driven Adaptive Visual Token Pruning for Efficient Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05950)

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出E-AdaPrune，一种基于能量驱动的自适应视觉令牌剪枝框架，通过奇异值谱分析动态确定令牌预算，在保持性能的同时加速视觉语言模型推理。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有视觉令牌剪枝方法通常采用固定预算策略，忽略了不同图像信息密度的显著差异，导致对信息稀疏图像的过度处理和信息密集图像的处理不足，限制了视觉语言模型的加速效率。

**Method:** E-AdaPrune框架通过分析视觉特征空间的奇异值谱，基于保留特定比例谱能量的原则动态确定令牌预算，为信息密集场景分配更多令牌同时压缩冗余内容，无需引入额外可学习参数，并采用随机奇异值分解控制计算开销。

**Result:** 在九个基准测试和三个VLM骨干网络上的评估表明，在匹配的平均令牌预算下，E-AdaPrune带来平均0.6%的性能提升，在MMVet推理任务上实现+5.1%的相对提升，同时每张图像的额外延迟仅8毫秒。

**Conclusion:** 该研究证明了基于谱能量的自适应令牌剪枝策略的有效性，为视觉语言模型的高效推理提供了参数无关的解决方案，同时保持甚至提升模型性能，为实际部署中的计算资源优化提供了新思路。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Visual token reduction is critical for accelerating Vision-Language Models (VLMs), yet most existing approaches rely on a fixed budget shared across all inputs, overlooking the substantial variation in image information density. We propose E-AdaPrune, an energy-driven adaptive pruning framework that determines the token budget from the singular value spectrum of the visual features space. By preserving a certain proportion of spectral energy, our method allocates more tokens to information-dense scenes while aggressively compressing redundant ones, without introducing additional learnable parameters. We evaluate E-AdaPrune on nine benchmarks and three VLM backbones, LLaVA-1.5-7B, LLaVA-1.5-13B, and LLaVA-NeXT-8B. Under matched average token budgets, E-AdaPrune consistently yields an average improvement of up to 0.6\%, including a significant +5.1\% relative boost on the MMVet reasoning task. Using randomized singular value decomposition, the additional latency is limited to 8ms per image.


### [25] [PatchCue: Enhancing Vision-Language Model Reasoning with Patch-Based Visual Cues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05869)
*Yukun Qi, Pei Fu, Hang Li, Yuhan Liu, Chao Jiang, Bin Qin, Zhenbo Luo, Jian Luan*

#### 🧩 TL;DR

**Method:** 本文提出PatchCue范式，通过将图像划分为补丁并在补丁级别表示视觉线索。采用两阶段训练方法：首先进行冷启动监督微调以输出补丁级提示，然后通过强化学习结合过程监督的提示奖励来引导中间视觉推理步骤。该方法充分利用了现代VLM的补丁标记化输入结构。

**Result:** 在多个VLM模型和多样化基准测试（包括通用视觉问答、复杂推理和文档理解）上的广泛实验表明，PatchCue能持续提升整体模型性能。结果显示补丁级提示在性能上优于像素级边界框和基于点的提示方法，为视觉推理提供了更有效的解决方案。

**Conclusion:** PatchCue提供了一种更有效且认知对齐的视觉推理范式，通过补丁级视觉提示显著增强了VLM的视觉推理能力。该方法不仅技术性能优越，而且更符合人类感知习惯，为未来多模态推理系统的设计提供了新的方向。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved remarkable progress on a wide range of challenging multimodal understanding and reasoning tasks. However, existing reasoning paradigms, such as the classical Chain-of-Thought (CoT), rely solely on textual information and often underutilize important visual cues. While prior work has incorporated pixel-level visual cues, these representations require precise spatial localization, introducing additional learning complexity. To address this, we propose PatchCue, a novel patch-based visual cue paradigm designed to significantly enhance the visual reasoning capabilities of VLMs. By partitioning images into patches and representing cues at the patch level, PatchCue aligns better with human perceptual habits and leverages the patch-tokenized input of modern VLMs. We train VLMs using a two-stage approach: cold-start supervised fine-tuning to output patch-level cues, followed by reinforcement learning with a process-supervised cue reward that guides intermediate visual reasoning steps. Extensive experiments on multiple VLMs and diverse benchmarks, including general visual question answering, complex reasoning, and document understanding, demonstrate that PatchCue consistently improves overall model performance. Our results show that patch-level cues outperform both pixel-level bounding boxes and point-based cues, providing a more effective and cognitively aligned visual reasoning paradigm.

#### 📄 Abstract
Irregularly sampled time series (ISTS) are widespread in real-world scenarios, exhibiting asynchronous observations on uneven time intervals across variables. Existing ISTS forecasting methods often solely utilize historical observations to predict future ones while falling short in learning contextual semantics and fine-grained temporal patterns. To address these problems, we achieve MM-ISTS, a multimodal framework augmented by vision-text large language models, that bridges temporal, visual, and textual modalities, facilitating ISTS forecasting. MM-ISTS encompasses a novel two-stage encoding mechanism. In addition, a multimodal alignment module with modality-aware gating is designed to alleviate the modality gap across ISTS, images, and text. **Method:** MemSeg-Agent采用记忆增强架构，将适应过程从权重空间转移到记忆空间，通过智能体控制器动态组合轻量级静态记忆、少样本记忆和测试时工作记忆来调节固定骨干网络，在联邦设置中更新紧凑的记忆单元而非模型参数。

**Conclusion:** MemSeg-Agent为可扩展和自适应的医学图像分割引入了新范式，在智能体AI时代实现了从权重空间适应到记忆空间适应的转变，为联邦学习中的高效知识共享和持续适应提供了可行方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Medical image segmentation is fundamental to clinical workflows, yet models trained on a single dataset often fail to generalize across institutions, scanners, or patient populations. While vision foundation models have shown great promise in addressing this challenge, their deployment typically requires task-specific fine-tuning, which introduces substantial communication overhead in federated learning and prevents continuous knowledge evolution during deployment. In this work, we propose a memory-augmented segmentation agent (MemSeg-Agent) that shifts adaptation from weight space to memory space, enabling few-shot learning, federated supervised learning, and test-time adaptation within a unified architecture. MemSeg-Agent conditions a fixed backbone with lightweight static, few-shot, and test-time working memories, which are dynamically composed by an agentic controller. In federated settings, we update compact memory units instead of model parameters, substantially reducing communication overhead. Experiments on four public datasets demonstrate strong performance and robustness to domain shift: Static memory alone matches or surpasses strong supervised baselines with high parameter efficiency, and test-time working memory further improves in-domain and cross-domain performance without fine-tuning. Overall, MemSeg-Agent introduces a new paradigm for scalable and adaptive medical image segmentation in the era of agentic AI.


### [28] [CylinderSplat: 3D Gaussian Splatting with Cylindrical Triplanes for Panoramic Novel View Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05882)
*Qiwei Wang, Xianghui Ze, Jingyi Yu, Yujiao Shi*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了CylinderSplat，一种用于全景3D高斯泼溅的前馈框架，通过引入圆柱形三平面表示和双分支架构，解决了现有方法在稀疏视图场景下的遮挡问题和全景数据几何表示不匹配的挑战。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有前馈3D高斯泼溅方法在全景图像应用中存在两个主要问题：基于多视图代价体积的几何细化方法在稀疏视图场景下难以解决遮挡问题，以及标准的笛卡尔三平面等体积表示无法有效捕捉360度场景的固有几何结构，导致失真和混叠现象。

**Method:** 本文提出了CylinderSplat框架，其核心创新是圆柱形三平面表示，该表示与全景数据及符合曼哈顿世界假设的真实世界结构更加匹配。采用双分支架构设计：像素分支负责重建观测良好的区域，而体积分支则利用圆柱形三平面来补全被遮挡或稀疏观测的区域。该框架能够灵活处理从单视图到多视图的变数量输入全景图像。

**Result:** 大量实验表明，CylinderSplat在单视图和多视图全景新视角合成任务中均取得了最先进的结果。该方法在重建质量和几何精度方面均优于先前方法，特别是在处理稀疏视图场景时表现出更强的鲁棒性和准确性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究证明了圆柱形三平面表示在全景3D重建中的有效性，为实时全景新视角合成提供了更优的解决方案。双分支架构的设计平衡了观测良好区域的重建质量与被遮挡区域的补全能力，为处理变数量输入视图的全景3DGS应用提供了灵活且高效的框架。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Feed-forward 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has shown great promise for real-time novel view synthesis, but its application to panoramic imagery remains challenging. Existing methods often rely on multi-view cost volumes for geometric refinement, which struggle to resolve occlusions in sparse-view scenarios. Furthermore, standard volumetric representations like Cartesian Triplanes are poor in capturing the inherent geometry of $360^\circ$ scenes, leading to distortion and aliasing.
  In this work, we introduce CylinderSplat, a feed-forward framework for panoramic 3DGS that addresses these limitations. The core of our method is a new {cylindrical Triplane} representation, which is better aligned with panoramic data and real-world structures adhering to the Manhattan-world assumption. We use a dual-branch architecture: a pixel-based branch reconstructs well-observed regions, while a volume-based branch leverages the cylindrical Triplane to complete occluded or sparsely-viewed areas. Our framework is designed to flexibly handle a variable number of input views, from single to multiple panoramas. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CylinderSplat achieves state-of-the-art results in both single-view and multi-view panoramic novel view synthesis, outperforming previous methods in both reconstruction quality and geometric accuracy.


### [29] [Probing Visual Concepts in Lightweight Vision-Language Models for Automated Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06054)
*Nikos Theodoridis, Reenu Mohandas, Ganesh Sistu, Anthony Scanlan, Ciarán Eising, Tim Brophy*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
该研究通过分析视觉语言模型（VLM）的中间激活，探究其在自动驾驶相关简单视觉任务上的失败原因，识别出感知失败和认知失败两种故障模式，并揭示了视觉概念在模型中的线性编码特性。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 视觉语言模型在自动驾驶应用中日益普及，旨在利用其推理和泛化能力处理长尾场景，但这些模型经常在自动驾驶高度相关的简单视觉问题上失败，且失败原因尚不明确，本研究旨在深入理解这些故障背后的机制。

**Method:** 研究通过创建仅针对特定视觉概念存在差异的反事实图像集，并训练线性探针来区分这些图像，分析四种最先进视觉语言模型的中间激活，评估特定视觉概念在线性编码中的程度，从而识别视觉信息流中的瓶颈。

**Result:** 实验发现物体或智能体存在等概念在模型激活中具有显式线性编码，而物体方向等空间视觉概念仅通过视觉编码器保留的空间结构隐式编码，研究识别出两种故障模式：感知失败（所需视觉信息未线性编码）和认知失败（视觉信息存在但未能与语言语义正确对齐），同时发现物体距离增加会快速降低相应视觉概念的线性可分性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究提高了对视觉语言模型在自动驾驶相关简单视觉任务上失败案例的理解，揭示了视觉概念在模型中的编码特性和两种不同的故障机制，为改进模型在关键应用中的可靠性提供了诊断框架和理论基础。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
The use of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) in automated driving applications is becoming increasingly common, with the aim of leveraging their reasoning and generalisation capabilities to handle long tail scenarios. However, these models often fail on simple visual questions that are highly relevant to automated driving, and the reasons behind these failures remain poorly understood. In this work, we examine the intermediate activations of VLMs and assess the extent to which specific visual concepts are linearly encoded, with the goal of identifying bottlenecks in the flow of visual information. Specifically, we create counterfactual image sets that differ only in a targeted visual concept and then train linear probes to distinguish between them using the activations of four state-of-the-art (SOTA) VLMs. Our results show that concepts such as the presence of an object or agent in a scene are explicitly and linearly encoded, whereas other spatial visual concepts, such as the orientation of an object or agent, are only implicitly encoded by the spatial structure retained by the vision encoder. In parallel, we observe that in certain cases, even when a concept is linearly encoded in the model's activations, the model still fails to answer correctly. This leads us to identify two failure modes. The first is perceptual failure, where the visual information required to answer a question is not linearly encoded in the model's activations. The second is cognitive failure, where the visual information is present but the model fails to align it correctly with language semantics. Finally, we show that increasing the distance of the object in question quickly degrades the linear separability of the corresponding visual concept. Overall, our findings improve our understanding of failure cases in VLMs on simple visual tasks that are highly relevant to automated driving.


### [30] [CollabOD: Collaborative Multi-Backbone with Cross-scale Vision for UAV Small Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05905)
*Xuecheng Bai, Yuxiang Wang, Chuanzhi Xu, Boyu Hu, Kang Han, Ruijie Pan, Xiaowei Niu, Xiaotian Guan, Liqiang Fu, Pengfei Ye*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出CollabOD，一种轻量级协作检测框架，通过结构细节保留、跨路径特征对齐和定位感知轻量化设计，解决无人机图像中小目标检测的尺度变化和细节退化问题，在保持高效推理的同时提升检测稳定性。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 无人机图像中的小目标检测面临尺度变化、结构细节退化和计算资源有限等挑战，特别是在高海拔场景中，细粒度特征在分层下采样和跨尺度融合过程中进一步减弱，导致定位不稳定和鲁棒性降低。

**Method:** 提出CollabOD轻量级协作检测框架，集成结构细节保留、跨路径特征对齐和定位感知轻量化设计策略，从图像处理、通道结构和轻量化设计角度优化传统无人机感知模型架构，并引入统一的细节感知检测头以提升回归鲁棒性。

**Result:** 所提框架在保持高效推理的同时增强了表示稳定性，统一的细节感知检测头在不引入额外部署开销的情况下进一步提高了回归鲁棒性，代码已在GitHub上开源供社区使用。

**Conclusion:** 该研究通过协同优化特征表示和计算效率，为无人机小目标检测提供了有效的解决方案，框架的设计理念可扩展到其他资源受限的视觉感知任务中，平衡了检测精度与计算开销的权衡。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Small object detection in unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) imagery is challenging, mainly due to scale variation, structural detail degradation, and limited computational resources. In high-altitude scenarios, fine-grained features are further weakened during hierarchical downsampling and cross-scale fusion, resulting in unstable localization and reduced robustness. To address this issue, we propose CollabOD, a lightweight collaborative detection framework that explicitly preserves structural details and aligns heterogeneous feature streams before multi-scale fusion. The framework integrates Structural Detail Preservation, Cross-Path Feature Alignment, and Localization-Aware Lightweight Design strategies. From the perspectives of image processing, channel structure, and lightweight design, it optimizes the architecture of conventional UAV perception models. The proposed design enhances representation stability while maintaining efficient inference. A unified detail-aware detection head further improves regression robustness without introducing additional deployment overhead. The code is available at: https://github.com/Bai-Xuecheng/CollabOD.


### [31] [Place-it-R1: Unlocking Environment-aware Reasoning Potential of MLLM for Video Object Insertion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06140)
*Bohai Gu, Taiyi Wu, Dazhao Du, Jian Liu, Shuai Yang, Xiaotong Zhao, Alan Zhao, Song Guo*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出Place-it-R1框架，通过利用多模态大语言模型的链式思维推理能力，实现物理一致的视频对象插入，解决了现有方法仅关注视觉保真度而忽视物理因果关系的局限性。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现代视频编辑技术在插入视频对象时虽能达到高视觉保真度，但主要关注视觉优化而非物理因果关系，导致编辑结果与环境的物理一致性不足，存在物理上不合理的插入问题。

**Method:** 提出端到端框架Place-it-R1，采用Think-then-Place范式，利用MLLM的链式思维推理协调视频扩散模型，包含三个关键创新：MLLM进行物理场景理解和交互推理生成环境感知的链式思维令牌并推断有效插入区域；引入MLLM引导的空间直接偏好优化，通过反馈评分机制确保视觉自然性；在推理时MLLM迭代触发细化循环并引导扩散模型进行自适应调整，形成闭环渐进式优化。

**Result:** 大量实验表明，Place-it-R1相比最先进的解决方案和商业模型，能够实现物理一致性的视频对象插入，显著提升了编辑结果的物理合理性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究展示了MLLM在连接认知推理与生成执行方面的潜力，通过闭环优化机制和用户可选的两种模式（合理性导向的灵活模式和保真度导向的标准模式），为视频编辑提供了物理一致性与视觉保真度之间的可控权衡。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Modern video editing techniques have achieved high visual fidelity when inserting video objects. However, they focus on optimizing visual fidelity rather than physical causality, leading to edits that are physically inconsistent with their environment. In this work, we present Place-it-R$1$, an end-to-end framework for video object insertion that unlocks the environment-aware reasoning potential of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs). Our framework leverages the Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning of MLLMs to orchestrate video diffusion, following a Think-then-Place paradigm. To bridge cognitive reasoning and generative execution, we introduce three key innovations: First, MLLM performs physical scene understanding and interaction reasoning, generating environment-aware chain-of-thought tokens and inferring valid insertion regions to explicitly guide the diffusion toward physically plausible insertion. Then, we introduce MLLM-guided Spatial Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), where diffusion outputs are fed back to the MLLM for scoring, enabling visual naturalness. During inference, the MLLM iteratively triggers refinement cycles and elicits adaptive adjustments from the diffusion model, forming a closed-loop that progressively enhances editing quality. Furthermore, we provide two user-selectable modes: a plausibility-oriented flexible mode that permits environment modifications (\eg, generating support structures) to enhance physical plausibility, and a fidelity-oriented standard mode that preserves scene integrity for maximum fidelity, offering users explicit control over the plausibility-fidelity trade-off. Extensive experiments demonstrate Place-it-R1 achieves physically-coherent video object insertion compared with state-of-the-art solutions and commercial models.


### [32] [VLM-RobustBench: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Robustness of Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06148)
*Rohit Saxena, Alessandro Suglia, Pasquale Minervini*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
该研究提出了VLM-RobustBench基准测试，系统评估了视觉语言模型在现实世界图像失真下的鲁棒性，发现当前模型在语义理解上表现强劲但对空间扰动脆弱，特别是重采样和几何失真会导致性能显著下降。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 尽管视觉语言模型在标准高质量数据集上表现优异，但对其在现实世界图像失真条件下的性能理解仍然不足，缺乏系统评估模型在各种图像扰动下鲁棒性的综合基准。

**Method:** 研究构建了VLM-RobustBench基准，涵盖噪声、模糊、天气、数字和几何五大类共49种增强类型，在分级严重程度（低/中/高）和二元变换下产生133个损坏设置，评估了来自四个模型家族（Qwen、InternVL、Molmo、Gemma）的VLM在两个互补基准（MMBench视觉基础和MMMU-Pro推理导向）上的表现。

**Result:** 实验结果显示视觉严重程度是性能下降的弱预测指标：低严重度的空间扰动通常比视觉上严重的光度损坏更降低性能，特别是低严重度的玻璃模糊使MMBench准确率平均下降约8个百分点，而重采样和几何失真（如上采样、弹性变换）导致最大降幅达34个百分点。

**Conclusion:** 当前视觉语言模型在语义理解上表现强劲但对空间扰动脆弱，这一发现强调了需要定义新的鲁棒性评估协议和训练机制，特别应关注重采样和几何不变性的增强，以提升模型在现实世界失真条件下的实际应用能力。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-language models (VLMs) achieve strong performance on standard, high-quality datasets, but we still do not fully understand how they perform under real-world image distortions. We present VLM-RobustBench, a benchmark spanning 49 augmentation types across noise, blur, weather, digital, and geometric perturbations, evaluated under graded severities (low/mid/high) and binary transforms, yielding 133 corrupted settings. We evaluate VLMs from four families (Qwen, InternVL, Molmo, Gemma) on two complementary benchmarks: MMBench (visually grounded) and MMMU-Pro (reasoning-oriented). Our results reveal that visual severity is a weak predictor of difficulty: low-severity spatial perturbations often degrade performance more than visually severe photometric corruptions. In particular, low-severity glass_blur reduces MMBench accuracy by about 8 pp on average across models, while the largest drops arise from resampling and geometric distortions (e.g., upsample, elastic_transform), reaching up to 34 pp. Overall, our findings suggest current VLMs are semantically strong but spatially fragile, motivating the definition of novel robustness evaluation protocols and training regimes that emphasize resampling and geometric invariances.


### [33] [Reflective Flow Sampling Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06165)
*Zikai Zhou, Muyao Wang, Shitong Shao, Lichen Bai, Haoyi Xiong, Bo Han, Zeke Xie*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了反射流采样（RF-Sampling），一种专为流匹配模型设计的免训练推理增强框架，通过理论推导证明其隐式执行文本-图像对齐分数的梯度上升，显著提升了FLUX等流模型的生成质量和提示对齐能力。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 当前推理时增强策略主要适用于传统扩散模型，但在流匹配模型（如FLUX）上表现不佳，这限制了流模型在文本到图像生成中的潜力，需要专门针对流模型设计的推理增强框架来填补这一技术空白。

**Method:** 提出了反射流采样（RF-Sampling），这是一种基于理论推导的免训练推理增强框架，专门为流模型特别是CFG蒸馏变体设计。该方法通过文本表示的线性组合与流反转技术相结合，使模型能够探索与输入提示更一致的噪声空间，其理论推导证明了该方法隐式执行文本-图像对齐分数的梯度上升。

**Result:** 在多个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，RF-Sampling能够持续提升生成质量和提示对齐能力，并且是首个在FLUX模型上展现出一定程度测试时缩放能力的推理增强方法，显著优于现有启发式方法在流模型上的表现。

**Conclusion:** 该研究为流匹配模型提供了首个专门设计的理论化推理增强框架，不仅填补了技术空白，还展示了流模型在推理时优化的潜力，为未来流模型的高质量生成开辟了新方向，同时证明了理论推导相对于启发式方法在复杂生成任务中的优越性。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
The growing demand for text-to-image generation has led to rapid advances in generative modeling. Recently, text-to-image diffusion models trained with flow matching algorithms, such as FLUX, have achieved remarkable progress and emerged as strong alternatives to conventional diffusion models. At the same time, inference-time enhancement strategies have been shown to improve the generation quality and text-prompt alignment of text-to-image diffusion models. However, these techniques are mainly applicable to conventional diffusion models and usually fail to perform well on flow models. To bridge this gap, we propose Reflective Flow Sampling (RF-Sampling), a theoretically-grounded and training-free inference enhancement framework explicitly designed for flow models, especially for the CFG-distilled variants (i.e., models distilled from CFG guidance techniques), like FLUX. Departing from heuristic interpretations, we provide a formal derivation proving that RF-Sampling implicitly performs gradient ascent on the text-image alignment score. By leveraging a linear combination of textual representations and integrating them with flow inversion, RF-Sampling allows the model to explore noise spaces that are more consistent with the input prompt. Extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that RF-Sampling consistently improves both generation quality and prompt alignment. Moreover, RF-Sampling is also the first inference enhancement method that can exhibit test-time scaling ability to some extent on FLUX.


### [34] [Towards Driver Behavior Understanding: Weakly-Supervised Risk Perception in Driving Scenes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05926)
*Nakul Agarwal, Yi-Ting Chen, Behzad Dariush*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了RAID数据集，这是一个专门用于驾驶员风险感知和上下文风险评估研究的大规模数据集，并在此基础上开发了一种弱监督风险对象识别框架，显著提升了风险识别性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 实现零碰撞移动性是智能车辆系统的关键目标，这需要理解驾驶员的风险感知——这是一个复杂的认知过程，受到驾驶员对外部刺激的自愿反应以及周围道路使用者对自车的关注度的影响。当前缺乏专门针对驾驶员风险感知和上下文风险评估的大规模数据集，限制了该领域的研究进展。

**Method:** 本文引入了RAID数据集，包含4,691个标注视频片段，涵盖多样化的交通场景，标注内容包括驾驶员的预期操作、道路拓扑、风险情况、驾驶员反应和行人注意力。基于该数据集，提出了一种弱监督风险对象识别框架，通过建模驾驶员预期操作与反应之间的关系来识别潜在风险源，并分析了行人注意力在风险评估中的作用。

**Result:** 实验评估表明，所提出的方法在RAID数据集上相比先前最先进方法实现了20.6%的性能提升，在HDDS数据集上实现了23.1%的性能提升。RAID数据集的有效性得到了验证，为驾驶员风险感知研究提供了有价值的资源。

**Conclusion:** RAID数据集填补了驾驶员风险感知研究领域的数据空白，提出的弱监督风险对象识别框架通过建模驾驶员行为与风险源之间的关系，显著提升了风险识别性能。该研究强调了上下文信息（如行人注意力）在风险评估中的重要性，为智能车辆系统的安全决策提供了新的视角和方法。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Achieving zero-collision mobility remains a key objective for intelligent vehicle systems, which requires understanding driver risk perception-a complex cognitive process shaped by voluntary response of the driver to external stimuli and the attentiveness of surrounding road users towards the ego-vehicle. To support progress in this area, we introduce RAID (Risk Assessment In Driving scenes)-a large-scale dataset specifically curated for research on driver risk perception and contextual risk assessment. RAID comprises 4,691 annotated video clips, covering diverse traffic scenarios with labels for driver's intended maneuver, road topology, risk situations (e.g., crossing pedestrians), driver responses, and pedestrian attentiveness. Leveraging RAID, we propose a weakly supervised risk object identification framework that models the relationship between driver's intended maneuver and responses to identify potential risk sources. Additionally, we analyze the role of pedestrian attention in estimating risk and demonstrate the value of the proposed dataset. Experimental evaluations demonstrate that our method achieves 20.6% and 23.1% performance gains over prior state-of-the-art approaches on the RAID and HDDS datasets, respectively.


### [35] [OD-RASE: Ontology-Driven Risk Assessment and Safety Enhancement for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05936)
*Kota Shimomura, Masaki Nambata, Atsuya Ishikawa, Ryota Mimura, Takayuki Kawabuchi, Takayoshi Yamashita, Koki Inoue*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出OD-RASE框架，通过检测导致交通事故的道路结构并将其与基础设施改进相连接，以增强自动驾驶系统的安全性。该框架结合领域本体论和大规模视觉语言模型，实现了对事故风险道路的主动识别与改进方案生成。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 当前自动驾驶系统在处理罕见情况或复杂道路结构时仍存在局限，而道路基础设施设计主要面向人类驾驶员且安全改进通常采取被动反应式方法。这种反应式方法对需要主动风险缓解的自动驾驶系统构成重大挑战，因此需要建立连接事故检测与基础设施开发的系统性框架。

**Method:** 研究提出OD-RASE框架，首先基于道路交通系统专业知识形式化本体论，同时利用大规模视觉语言模型生成基础设施改进方案，并通过本体驱动数据过滤增强可靠性。框架还包括OD-RASE模型，结合LVLM和扩散模型生成改进方案及改进后道路环境的生成图像，构建了新的数据集。

**Result:** 实验表明本体驱动数据过滤能够高精度预测导致事故的道路结构及相应改进计划。该方法实现了对事故前道路图像的自动标注，成功构建了包含基础设施改进提案的新数据集，验证了框架在连接事故检测与基础设施开发方面的有效性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究为交通环境整体安全性做出贡献，标志着向更广泛采用自动驾驶系统迈出重要一步。提出的主动风险缓解方法超越了传统反应式安全改进，通过系统化连接事故分析与基础设施规划，为自动驾驶安全提供了新的范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Although autonomous driving systems demonstrate high perception performance, they still face limitations when handling rare situations or complex road structures. Such road infrastructures are designed for human drivers, safety improvements are typically introduced only after accidents occur. This reactive approach poses a significant challenge for autonomous systems, which require proactive risk mitigation. To address this issue, we propose OD-RASE, a framework for enhancing the safety of autonomous driving systems by detecting road structures that cause traffic accidents and connecting these findings to infrastructure development. First, we formalize an ontology based on specialized domain knowledge of road traffic systems. In parallel, we generate infrastructure improvement proposals using a large-scale visual language model (LVLM) and use ontology-driven data filtering to enhance their reliability. This process automatically annotates improvement proposals on pre-accident road images, leading to the construction of a new dataset. Furthermore, we introduce the Baseline approach (OD-RASE model), which leverages LVLM and a diffusion model to produce both infrastructure improvement proposals and generated images of the improved road environment. Our experiments demonstrate that ontology-driven data filtering enables highly accurate prediction of accident-causing road structures and the corresponding improvement plans. We believe that this work contributes to the overall safety of traffic environments and marks an important step toward the broader adoption of autonomous driving systems.


### [36] [SLER-IR: Spherical Layer-wise Expert Routing for All-in-One Image Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05940)
*Peng Shurui, Xin Lin, Shi Luo, Jincen Ou, Dizhe Zhang, Lu Qi, Truong Nguyen, Chao Ren*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出SLER-IR，一种球面分层专家路由框架，通过动态激活跨网络层的专用专家来解决统一图像恢复中的特征干扰和专家专业化不足问题，在多项任务基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 统一的一体化图像恢复框架在处理多样化退化时面临特征干扰和专家专业化不足的挑战，现有方法难以在统一架构中有效处理不同类型的图像退化问题。

**Method:** 提出球面分层专家路由框架SLER-IR，包含球面均匀退化嵌入和对比学习，将退化表示映射到超球面以消除线性嵌入空间的几何偏差；同时设计全局-局部粒度融合模块，整合全局语义和局部退化线索以处理空间非均匀退化和训练-测试粒度差距。

**Result:** 在三任务和五任务基准测试中，SLER-IR在PSNR和SSIM指标上均优于现有最先进方法，实现了持续的性能改进，证明了该框架在处理多样化图像退化任务中的有效性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究展示了通过球面退化表示和分层专家路由机制可以有效解决统一图像恢复中的特征干扰问题，为处理多样化退化任务提供了一种新的架构设计思路，未来可扩展到更广泛的图像处理任务中。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Image restoration under diverse degradations remains challenging for unified all-in-one frameworks due to feature interference and insufficient expert specialization. We propose SLER-IR, a spherical layer-wise expert routing framework that dynamically activates specialized experts across network layers. To ensure reliable routing, we introduce a Spherical Uniform Degradation Embedding with contrastive learning, which maps degradation representations onto a hypersphere to eliminate geometry bias in linear embedding spaces. In addition, a Global-Local Granularity Fusion (GLGF) module integrates global semantics and local degradation cues to address spatially non-uniform degradations and the train-test granularity gap. Experiments on three-task and five-task benchmarks demonstrate that SLER-IR achieves consistent improvements over state-of-the-art methods in both PSNR and SSIM. Code and models will be publicly released.


### [37] [DeepSight: Bridging Depth Maps and Language with a Depth-Driven Multimodal Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06090)
*Hao Yang, Hongbo Zhang, Yanyan Zhao, Bing Qin*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了DeepSight，首个专门用于深度感知的多模态大语言模型，通过利用深度图像的独特特性增强三维场景理解能力，显著提升了深度感知和下游任务性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 当前多模态大语言模型在图像描述和视觉问答等任务上表现优异，但往往难以准确解释视觉数据中的深度信息，这限制了三维场景理解能力，因此需要专门针对深度感知设计的模型来解决这一局限性。

**Method:** DeepSight采用创新的深度图像处理方法，构建了新颖的深度图像-文本对数据集和深度指令数据集，使用GLPN模型从视觉图像生成深度图，并利用GPT-4策划相应的深度指令。同时修改CLIP中的ViT编码器以纳入局部物体信息，更有效地捕捉深度的细微连续变化。

**Result:** 实验结果表明，DeepSight在基于现有深度图像数据集构建的全面深度问答基准测试中表现优异，显著增强了深度感知能力和下游任务性能，验证了该模型在三维理解方面的有效性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究标志着多模态三维理解领域的重要进展，证明了专门针对深度感知设计的MLLM能够有效解决传统模型在深度信息解释方面的不足，为未来三维场景理解研究提供了新的方向和方法论基础。
